-pop                  : Population distribution and intra-partition visit order
-insert               : Insert specific options relating to various methods for batching and splitting partition updates

-schema               : Replication settings, compression, compaction, etc.

-transport            : Custom transport factories
-port                 : The port to connect to cassandra nodes on

-graph                : Graph recorded metrics
-tokenrange           : Token range settings

Connected to Test Cluster at 127.0.0.1:9042
[cqlsh 6.0.0 | Cassandra 4.0.13 | CQL spec 3.4.5 | Native protocol v5]
Use HELP for help.
cqlsh> describe keyspaces;

example    system       system_distributed  system_traces  system_virtual_schema
keyspace1  system_auth  system_schema       system_views   tagging

cqlsh> describe keyspace tagging;

CREATE KEYSPACE tagging WITH replication = {'class': 'SimpleStrategy', 'replication_factor': '1'}  AND durable_writes = true;

CREATE TABLE tagging.tag_entities (
    tag_id uuid,
    entity_id uuid,
    PRIMARY KEY (tag_id, entity_id)
) WITH CLUSTERING ORDER BY (entity_id ASC)
    AND additional_write_policy = '99p'
    AND bloom_filter_fp_chance = 0.01
    AND caching = {'keys': 'ALL', 'rows_per_partition': 'NONE'}
    AND cdc = false
    AND comment = ''
    AND compaction = {'class': 'org.apache.cassandra.db.compaction.SizeTieredCompactionStrategy', 'max_threshold': '32', 'min_threshold': '4'}
    AND compression = {'chunk_length_in_kb': '16', 'class': 'org.apache.cassandra.io.compress.LZ4Compressor'}
    AND crc_check_chance = 1.0
    AND default_time_to_live = 0
    AND extensions = {}
    AND gc_grace_seconds = 864000
    AND max_index_interval = 2048
    AND memtable_flush_period_in_ms = 0
    AND min_index_interval = 128
    AND read_repair = 'BLOCKING'
    AND speculative_retry = '99p';

CREATE TABLE tagging.tags (
    id uuid PRIMARY KEY,
    description text,
    name text,
    owner_id int,
    properties text
) WITH additional_write_policy = '99p'
    AND bloom_filter_fp_chance = 0.01
    AND caching = {'keys': 'ALL', 'rows_per_partition': 'NONE'}
    AND cdc = false
    AND comment = ''
    AND compaction = {'class': 'org.apache.cassandra.db.compaction.SizeTieredCompactionStrategy', 'max_threshold': '32', 'min_threshold': '4'}
    AND compression = {'chunk_length_in_kb': '16', 'class': 'org.apache.cassandra.io.compress.LZ4Compressor'}
